< Text>
2 stars. The front desk staff is excellent. They are friendly, kind and care about the service they provide. I did not have a great experience with anything else. I dropped my laptop off early on a Tuesday, around 10 am. I was told 2-3 business days for turn around and diagnostic. I emailed on the third day as I hadn't heard anything yet and they responded a few hours later asking me to give them up to 4 business days. So on Friday, the fourth business day I got an email about 2 hours before closing from my tech, he had just started looking at my laptop at the end of the day on Friday. He explained it was an issue with my hard drive and I had provided a replacement drive to use. He said he would have it ready by End of day for me. He didn't contact me again for the remainder of my service time. I went in at 4:30 pm on Friday just before closing to ensure he had as much time as possible to perform the service on my laptop and repair the hard drive. when I got there he had left already and I couldn't get my device back when I requested it because it couldn't be found. They asked me to wait until Monday and told me it would be done first thing Monday morning and I would have it no later than noon. So I sent an email Monday, 6 days after I dropped off my computer originally. A bit longer than 2-3 days. And my tech didn't respond to me at all. I went into the shop at 1:30 pm to check since I wasn't getting a response and again my tech was out and not working on my computer and it wasn't ready for pickup. They told me it would be done by 3:00 pm. I returned at 3:45 again giving them extra time from when they said to make sure it would be done and it wasn't. I waited in the lobby for a half hour for him to finish and then got a huge bill for a "windows reinstallation" which isn't what I needed done in the first place and I had explained when I dropped it off that I already had a new copy of windows to install myself and just needed my other hard drive installed and RAID setup. I had to do raid setup myself when I got home. $200 and a week gets you multiple trips to the store and a hard drive screwed into place. <text>Ok, first off, just telling you how awesome and big this was is impossible so the photo is for scale.

I ordered the Chicken Teriyaki Bowl. That's the small portion... Let me say that again, pictured is the small portion, and it's $5. The large portion items are $7, and I saw one, it's easily twice the size. My girlfriend ordered the Sweet & Sour Chicken, just as big and very yummy. We also got a Ebi Roll, and a Spicy Tuna Roll, all top shelf items with out question.  My only grip is no soda fountain, so we had to get Snapple. But all of that, 2 bowls, 2 rolls, and 2 drinks. $28. I can not tell you how good this food was for the price.

On our way out, we decided heck with it, lets get a smoothie. They are like $3.50 for a small, which is the perfect size. I had a banana and my gf had a mango. It tasted like they just crammed a ton of fruit in there. It was heavy like a milk shake, and tasted like heaven. Soo amazing, and I know I will be showing up again when the weather starts to get warm, like it already is. They do have a large version of the smoothies, and I think thy were like $4.50 or so, and the sign says 64oz, but I saw a few people order them, I think the sign lies, they were HUGE!!! Soo worth it.

In conclusion:
The scary part about this place is how good and cheap it is. It's also right next to the house, just as close as McD's, and basically the same price for a simple meal.<//text><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMSNGLbYAzrEFqFEyksnJ3Inv7Q521-fQWDCdQu=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics><response>None<//response>< GmapID>

< Review>
Repeatedly delighted.

I have had nothing but really excellent experiences with JetBlue.

The first time was on a delayed flight where I ran to Johnny Rockets in the terminal to get some chicken nuggets and I waited too long to order knowing that the plane was gonna board at any minute. I hoped that the food would be done but the pager never went off. Sadly, I walked to the gate and gave the gate attendant the pager and let him know that lunch is on me. After getting settled - probably 15 minutes after boarding into the plane and right before the doors closed, I see the desk attendant, looking for...Me - with my food! Man it made my day 100%.  I got a $25 credit for the delay too!

Today, I had to catch a flight to FLL and I didn't have my boarding pass yet. The nice lady gave me a really nice seat and I used my JetBlue plus card to waive the luggage fees.

I guess just deep down I appreciate that JetBlue seems to care. I hope they expand their flightpaths cuz I'm I might be some shade of trueblue for life.< /Review>

<UserId.>115069345271695915689< /UserId.>< name>
S Lee</name>
< Date>
1583304610367<//Date>
<Rating>4</Rating>< review>
I was in the Civic Center area tight on time and looking for a quick bite to eat before seeing Hamilton at the Orpheum Theater. Fortunately, I  happened upon Gyro King, and indeed this restaurant turned out to be the perfect solution! They have a very solid selection of gyro plates and wraps, which also includes a good variety of vegetation selections. The service is relatively quick, since all the food is pre-cooked and they simply need to assemble your plate/wrap before you can dig in and enjoy! The seating inside is a little tight, but I had no problems finding a table and they also offer outside seating if it does get full.

Before I get into the food, I will have to admit that the restaurant's location isn't in the most ideal place. There is a chance one could feel a little cautious eating in this area, but nevertheless it's a solid option for a fast meal in the Civic Area. You definitely can't go wrong with their food!

I ordered the lab and beef gyro plate, which also came with a serving of bread. Luckily, I was particularly hungry on this day or else I don't think I would've been able to finish it all off. They definitely give generous portions, so I hope you're hungry when you visit Gyro King (or at least bring a friend with you to share)!<//review>

< Text>
A great place to try something different. They serve chicken, beef and lamb as well as baclava. There's a small counter to sit at if you're alone, or you can opt to sit at one of the tables present (seating for 2 to 6 people). Wraps or plates, it won't matter; the food is plentiful and delicious. Beef and chicken are cheaper than lamb, so if you're looking to dine a la Bo Peep, get the lamb-only skewers.< /Text>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
Owners are so helpful, and food is prepared quickly tho it's all made from scratch. Prices are good for SF. Try the gyro or lamb shish-ka-bob. Their appetizer plate and side of hummus are very tasty, bread is fresh and any salad you get is going to be mouth-watering.

I grab my lunch to go often from their for a shift at Bill Graham, I'm often in a rush and I work the late shift from 5p-12p. I grab a combo gyro around 4:45, never have to wait and I'm good for the night. I brought my family in on Monday late afternoon and they really enjoyed it. The kids are sweet fiends do getting them to eat healthy is a chore, but they enjoyed this. We did have a piece of baklava and some rice pudding, it was fabulous.

A must do for anyone, visitor or local alike will truly enjoy the fare and the service.</review>
